{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-09-01 09:52:34","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 09:52:34","title":"Inspiration: Creative Portrait Illustration","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/inspiration-creative-portrait-illustration--cms-35510","description":"<p>One of the best ways to get your creative juices flowing is to look at a wide variety of art and think about what the artist is trying to communicate and how they use the techniques and tools at their disposal.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Portrait Illustration from Mixkit\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/woman-standing-behind-bright-leaves-and-plants-191-original.jpg\"><figcaption>In this post, you'll discover dozens of beautiful portrait illustrations like this one from <a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/woman-standing-behind-bright-leaves-and-plants-191/\" target=\"_self\">Mixkit</a><br></figcaption></figure><p>In this post, I'll share a wide cross-section of portrait illustrations to get you excited about creating projects, and I'll link to some tutorials in which you can learn how to create portraits of your own.</p><p>Ready to be inspired? Then let's begin.</p><h2>Portrait Illustration Inspiration From Envato Elements</h2><p>Envato Elements offers a huge range of <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/graphics/illustrations/portrait\" target=\"_self\">traditional illustration portraits</a> as well as more creative, experimental pieces. Here's a quick selection to excite and motivate, challenge and comfort.<br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/male-portrait-LNCGT3C\" target=\"_self\">Male Portrait Illustration</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/male-portrait-LNCGT3C\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Male Portrait Illustration\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/Male_Portrait_illustration.jpg\"></a></figure><p>A portrait is a collaboration between artist and subject and thus reflects something essential about both parties. Why has the artist chosen this colour palette? Does it reflect something they saw in the subject or something they felt within themselves? What did the artist want to communicate by juxtaposing sharp angles in the subject's neck, jaw and hair with the tenderness in the eyes and soft sensuality of the lips? What does this portrait make you feel?</p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/pregnant-woman-vector-illustration-RTEBTL6\" target=\"_self\">Stylized Portrait Illustration of a Pregnant Woman</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/pregnant-woman-vector-illustration-RTEBTL6\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Stylized Portrait Illustration of a Pregnant Woman\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/Portrait-Illustration_Pregnant-Woman.png\"></a></figure><p>Freedom of expression is essential to the creator, and no less so in portraiture, where the pressure to honour facts and details can stifle and hamper communication. In portraiture, therefore, it's critical to guard one's creative instincts—the instinct that guides one about what to include or exclude. You'd expect a \"faceless\" illustration to lack emotion, but this artist in following their instinct to exclude facial details relied on other strategies to communicate the vulnerability, tenderness, protectiveness and joy of motherhood: gesture, line, colour, shape.</p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/holy-muerte-woman-RFQQNMN\" target=\"_self\">Holy Muerte Portrait Illustration</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/holy-muerte-woman-RFQQNMN\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Holy Muerte Portrait Illustration\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/Holy-Muerte-Portrait.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Mexico's \"Day of the Dead\" creates endless possibilities for creative expression thanks to its fascinating juxtaposition of the joyful and the macabre. Though there is a tradition of technique, pattern, motifs, etc. in this type of portraiture that each artist must adhere to, there is still so much room for individual interpretation and expression. This is what keeps the tradition fresh and endlessly exciting. <br></p><h3><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/young-couple-making-self-portrait-vector-HJFSGF\" target=\"_self\">Young Couple Self Portrait Illustration</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/young-couple-making-self-portrait-vector-HJFSGF\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Young Couple Self Portrait Illustration\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/Self-Portrait-Illustration-Couple.png\"></a></figure><p>Bringing the childlike into the adult sphere has been more popular in the 21st century than at any other time in human history. Rich fodder for psychologists and social historians no doubt, and endlessly cute and comforting for many. This cartoon-inspired vector portrait eschews the Disney-style wide-eyed innocence for small, thin lines for the eyes, which works well to communicate the joy and sweetness of this self-portrait illustration. <br></p><h3><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/six-portraits-vector-illustration-red-and-black-SGJXQNU\" target=\"_self\">Red and Black Portraits</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/six-portraits-vector-illustration-red-and-black-SGJXQNU\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Red and Black Portraits\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/six-portraits.png\"></a></figure><p>Abstraction in portraiture is another way to communicate a variety of complex emotions and evoke a wide range of responses. With a handful of repeated and reinterpreted geometric shapes and a limited colour palette, this artist has managed to create a bold and commanding collection of portraits. <br></p><h2>Portrait Illustration Inspiration From GraphicRiver</h2><p>There are also loads of riveting portraits to be found at GraphicRiver, with thousands of <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/vectors/characters/people\" target=\"_self\">vector portrait illustrations</a> to browse. Here are some of the best options.</p><h3><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/muslim-girl-in-hijab/10457072\" target=\"_self\">Portrait Illustration of a Woman in Hijab</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/muslim-girl-in-hijab/10457072\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Portrait Illustration of a Woman in Hijab\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/35510/image/graphicriver-PBp2ZTpa-muslim-girl-in-hijab-inline-image-preview-source%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>This portrait is rendered with so much detail that it could almost pass for a photo. In a traditional illustration portrait, you can reach a high level of realism, while also being totally free to create the look you want. The best of both worlds! <br></p><h3><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/bearded-hipster-man-portrait-pointing-finger/20406709\" target=\"_self\">Hipster Pop Art Portrait Illustration</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/bearded-hipster-man-portrait-pointing-finger/20406709\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Hipster Pop Art Portrait Illustration\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/35510/image/graphicriver-bXfzDv7w-bearded-hipster-man-portrait-pointing-finger-inline-image-preview-source%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>One of the great things about portraiture that we hope we are capturing in this article is the range of styles possible within this one genre. This piece borrows from the Pop Art style of the 1960s, while updating it with a more contemporary hipster look to create the same sense of irony. <br></p><h3><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/parents-playing-with-their-kids/8526971\" target=\"_self\">Family Portrait Illustration of Parents Playing With Their Kids</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/parents-playing-with-their-kids/8526971\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Family Portrait Illustration of Parents Playing With Their Kids\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/35510/image/graphicriver-xeX38n9t-parents-playing-with-their-kids-inline-image-preview-source%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Art is a great vehicle for furthering social justice. This piece does that very well by capturing a same-sex couple and their children in an idealised cartoon-style family portrait illustration. Why? Because families come in all combinations.<br></p><h3><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/portrait-of-a-ghost-girl-in-the-cemetery/23683474\" target=\"_self\">Portrait of a Ghost Girl in the Cemetery</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/portrait-of-a-ghost-girl-in-the-cemetery/23683474\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Portrait of a Ghost Girl in the Cemetery\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/35510/image/graphicriver-NNmtnQAx-portrait-of-a-ghost-girl-in-the-cemetery-inline-image-preview-source%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Portrait illustrations can veer into the realm of fantasy any time you want! This haunting illustration blends the subject with the background and makes the whole scene merge together to communicate the ethereal nature of a lost, mournful ghost.<br></p><h3><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/young-smiling-family/26469170\" target=\"_self\">Young Smiling Family Portrait Illustration</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/young-smiling-family/26469170\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Young Smiling Family Portrait Illustration\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/35510/image/graphicriver-hiV5ccKC-young-smiling-family-inline-image-preview-source%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Here's another family portrait illustration, but this time it looks more like a posed studio photograph, with the subjects smiling for the camera. The way they're standing so close, with the mother cradling her daughter in her arms and the child holding onto her mother's neck, makes it clear that this is a loving family.<br></p><h2>Portrait Illustration Inspiration From Placeit</h2><p>Placeit is a useful online tool to help you create banners, T-shirt designs, mockups, and more—right in your web browser! It doesn't specialise in portrait illustration, but it does have a few great examples to help you get inspired for your next project:</p><h3><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/quote-t-shirt-design-generator-with-a-portrait-of-a-woman-2405c\" target=\"_self\">The Future Is Now</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/quote-t-shirt-design-generator-with-a-portrait-of-a-woman-2405c\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"The Future Is Now\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/portrait-of-a-woman-2405c.png\"></a></figure><p>The flat style of illustration gained popularity a few years ago, and this is a great example of the style, with its simple flat shapes and long shadows. The style is somewhat deceptive—although it looks very simple, pulling off a successful illustration is not as straightforward as you might think.<br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-t-shirt-design-template-featuring-an-artist-s-portrait-2606d\" target=\"_self\">Portrait Illustration for a Hip Hop T-Shirt</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/hip-hop-t-shirt-design-template-featuring-an-artist-s-portrait-2606d\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Portrait Illustration for a Hip Hop T-Shirt\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/hip-hop-t-shirt-design-template-featuring-an-artist-s-portrait-2606d.jpg\"></a></figure><p>This is billed as a T-shirt design, but it could also work as an album cover—stylized portrait illustrations like this one are very flexible and very on trend in the art world! They take their inspiration from snapshot photography, where the subject is captured in candid posture rather than posed. This brings a fresh dynamism to illustration. <br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-an-anarchist-ninja-3084a\" target=\"_self\">Portrait Illustration of an Anarchist Ninja</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-an-anarchist-ninja-3084a\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\" Portrait Illustration of an Anarchist Ninja\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-an-anarchist-ninja-3084a.jpg\"></a></figure><p>How about something a bit more edgy? This is such a striking portrait, with the folded arms, crossed swords, and the face obscured by mask and reflective goggles. Even if Anarchy weren't written below the illustration, it would still communicate a certain sense of threat.<br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-an-intellectual-looking-woman-illustration-2624d\" target=\"_self\">Living My Best Life</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-an-intellectual-looking-woman-illustration-2624d\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Living My Best Life portrait\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-an-intellectual-looking-woman-illustration-2624d.jpg\"></a></figure><p>We all want to live our best life, don't we? This is a great example of vector portraiture—just a few lines manage to communicate a sense of thoughtful yearning that fits the style of portrait perfectly. </p><h3><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/trendy-t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-anime-styled-female-characters-2395\" target=\"_self\">Anime Stylized Portrait Illustration for a T-Shirt Design</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/design-templates/stages/trendy-t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-anime-styled-female-characters-2395\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\" Anime Stylized Portrait Illustration\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/trendy-t-shirt-design-maker-featuring-anime-styled-female-characters-2395.jpg\"></a></figure><p>There's a lot going on in this Japanese-influenced design, but at the heart of it is the portrait of a young woman, again with an interesting pose, half-turning as if she's just heard us call out to her. The grid is an unusual background choice, but works thanks to the fluidity of the rest of the portrait.<br></p><h2>Portrait Illustration Inspiration From Mixkit</h2><p>Mixkit offers a small but high-quality selection of <a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/discover/people/\" target=\"_self\">creative portrait illustrations</a> by talented artists from around the world. And the best part is, they're completely free to download! Here are some examples.</p><h3><a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/woman-standing-behind-bright-leaves-and-plants-191/\" target=\"_self\">Woman Standing Behind Bright Leaves and Plants</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/woman-standing-behind-bright-leaves-and-plants-191/\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Woman Standing Behind Bright Leaves and Plants\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/woman-standing-behind-bright-leaves-and-plants-191-original.jpg\"></a></figure><p>This highly stylized portrait illustration is all about being at one with nature. There is no star here. The woman and the beautiful leaves that surround her work together to create a harmonious whole. <br></p><h3><a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/tired-person-sitting-on-an-empty-train-68/\" target=\"_self\">Tired Person Sitting on an Empty Train</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/tired-person-sitting-on-an-empty-train-68/\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Tired Person Sitting on an Empty Train\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/tired-person-sitting-on-an-empty-train-68-original.jpg\"></a></figure><p>While some portraits focus on a single person, others are more documentary and depict a person in the context of a whole scene. This one uses a stylised depiction of the interior of a bus at night to create a mood of isolation, fatigue, and loneliness. It's another example of communicating mood in portraiture without many facial details.<br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/person-with-brightly-colored-shapes-exploding-out-of-both-ears-129/\" target=\"_self\">Stylized Portrait Illustration of a Person With Brightly Colored Shapes</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/person-with-brightly-colored-shapes-exploding-out-of-both-ears-129/\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Stylized Portrait Illustration of a Person With Brightly Colored Shapes\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/person-with-brightly-colored-shapes-exploding-out-of-both-ears-129-original.jpg\"></a></figure><p>What makes this portrait so effective is the contrast between the black and white subject and the brightly coloured shapes exploding from their ears. This surreal scene is compounded by the troubled expression on the subject's face. In totality, a disturbing and fascinating portrait. </p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/man-sitting-in-front-of-a-fire-reading-from-a-66/\" target=\"_self\">Man Sitting in Front of a Fire, Reading From a Tablet</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/man-sitting-in-front-of-a-fire-reading-from-a-66/\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Man Sitting in Front of a Fire Reading From a Tablet\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/_man-sitting-in-front-of-a-fire-reading-from-a-66-original.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Colour is a powerful language for artists, and this portrait achieves its power and drama through its use of colour. The shades of blue contrast beautifully with the shades of pink, making the fire and the man stand out from the rest. The light coming from the tablet screen onto the subject's face is a nice touch too.<br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/happy-couple-with-their-small-dog-155/\" target=\"_self\">Family Portrait Illustration of a Happy Couple and a Dog</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://mixkit.co/free-stock-art/happy-couple-with-their-small-dog-155/\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Family Portrait Illustration of a Happy Couple and a Dog\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/happy-couple-with-their-small-dog-155-original.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Unexpected design choices can help make a portrait successful. This striking family portrait illustration is a great example of that because the people are upside down so that we can't quite read their faces easily, making them peripheral. Meanwhile, the dog, who is in the centre of the portrait and is the right way up, becomes the focal point. <br></p><h2>Portrait Illustration Inspiration From Envato Tuts+</h2><p>After more than a decade of teaching <a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/search/portrait+illustration\" target=\"_self\">portrait illustration</a> here on Envato Tuts+, we've got plenty of wonderful portraits to share with you. Here's just a small selection.<br></p><h3><a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/create-an-art-nouveau-inspired-glinda-character-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-24890\" target=\"_self\">Traditional Illustration Portrait in Art Nouveau Style</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/create-an-art-nouveau-inspired-glinda-character-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-24890\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Traditional Illustration Portrait in Art Nouveau Style\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/glinda.jpg\"></a></figure><p>When you're creating an illustration, it's a great chance to mix and match different styles and shed new light on familiar subjects. In this one, Glinda from <em>The Wizard of Oz</em> is given a fabulous Art Nouveau makeover. The Good Witch of the North has never looked so good!<br></p><h3><a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-set-of-veil-and-hijab-avatars-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-28482\" target=\"_self\">Set of 8 Veil and Hijab Illustrations</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-set-of-veil-and-hijab-avatars-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-28482\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Set of 8 Veil and Hijab Illustrations\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/00_Tut_May_2017_Hijab_Avatars_misschatz.jpg\"></a></figure><p>You can also use a single portrait illustration to create multiple variations. If you look closely, you'll see that all eight of these portraits are based on the same basic illustration, but the end results are all quite different.<br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-yoga-goddess-illustration-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-22791\" target=\"_self\">Yoga Goddess Stylized Portrait Illustration</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-yoga-goddess-illustration-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-22791\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Yoga Goddess Stylized Portrait Illustration\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/Yoga-Goddess-Portrait-Illustration.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Portraiture can also help you explore other cultures and traditions, as artist Asher Benson did in this striking yoga goddess portrait. Again we have an interesting pose at the heart of this portrait, but it's the wealth of fascinating details that really make it come alive.<br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-chibi-lollipop-and-lullaby-munchkin-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-24923\" target=\"_self\">Chibi Lollipop and Lullaby Munchkin</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-chibi-lollipop-and-lullaby-munchkin-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-24923\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Chibi Lollipop and Lullaby Munchkin\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/lullaby.jpg\"></a></figure><p>With illustration, the only limit is your imagination. This fantasy scene is a long way from a traditional illustration portrait. It takes us to an invented world of lollipops, rainbows, and so much more. What kind of world do you want to invent? <br></p><h3>\n<a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-spring-themed-illustration-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-28413\" target=\"_self\">Spring Portrait Illustration</a><br>\n</h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-spring-themed-illustration-in-adobe-illustrator--cms-28413\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Spring Portrait Illustration\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/48/posts/35510/image/spring-girl-01.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Let's finish up with something fun. This sweet illustration communicates the essence of spring through the flowers and birds in the woman's hair, and her expression also conveys the optimism that the season often inspires.<br></p><h2>Learn More About Portrait Illustration!</h2><p>I hope this article has given you plenty of inspiration and ideas to help you get started as an illustrator. sers/33/posts/29782/preview_image/ivprevie.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn82@2020_2/2020/09/01/01-52-46-177_ee58f8f845e9791e.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/980/posts/31587/preview_image/prevewl-rock_boy.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn71@2020_4/2020/09/01/01-52-47-983_f67738f46f87a4a0.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/33/posts/28886/preview_image/hairpreview.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn54@2020_1/2020/09/01/01-52-37-783_f8477c29ee1f7767.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/33/posts/14869/preview_image/curlyhairpreview.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn93@2020_3/2020/09/01/01-52-43-643_46172e833d1311b3.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/legacy-courses/CRS-98723.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn71@2020_4/2020/09/01/01-52-42-808_b8efd12141fb9c26.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/71/courses/399/preview_image/Malevector.jpg":null,"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/71/courses/663/preview_image/LineArt400x277.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn40@2020_1/2020/09/01/01-52-42-416_d13a60bb653465fc.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/71/courses/361/preview_image/AdvVectorPortrait.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn91@2020_1/2020/09/01/01-52-44-606_8f9a16b5b485578f.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/71/courses/444/preview_image/advvmanip.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn31@2020_2/2020/09/01/01-52-42-455_10125cacd2712fa1.webp","http://audio.tutsplus.com.feedsportal.com/c/35227/f/668805/s/35510/sc/4/mf.gif":null,"http://da.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/35510/a2.img":null,"http://pi.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/35510/a2t.img":null},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598925154482},{"createdTime":"2020-09-01 09:52:34","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 09:52:34","title":"How to Create a Party Flyer Template PSD in Photoshop","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-create-a-party-flyer-template-psd-in-photoshop--cms-35524","description":"<figure class=\"final-product final-product--image\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/final_image/final-product.jpg\" alt=\"Final product image\"><!--googleoff: index--><figcaption>What You'll Be Creating</figcaption><!--googleon: index--></figure><p>In this tutorial, you will learn how to create a party flyer template PSD design in Photoshop. I will explain everything in so much detail that everyone can create the effect, even those who have just opened Photoshop for the first time.</p><h2>What You Will Learn in This Party Flyer Template Tutorial<br>\n</h2><ul>\n<li>How to design a party flyer PSD template in Photoshop</li>\n<li>How to create guidelines for a Photoshop template</li>\n<li>How to add an explosive effect to a photo with a Photoshop action<br>\n</li>\n<li>Tips on designing a Photoshop flyer template </li>\n</ul><h2>What You'll Need</h2><p>To recreate the design above, you will need the following resources:</p><ul>\n<li>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/expessive-modern-dance-pose-WT4LEHF\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Stock Image 1</a>\n</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/girls-making-selfie-portrait-at-party-42RC9ZB\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Stock Image 2</a></li>\n<li>\n<a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/energy-photoshop-action-WHRLM97\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Energy Photoshop Action</a><br>\n</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://fonts.google.com/specimen/Fira+Sans\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Font 1</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/golden-arrow-classy-modern-geometric-font-KBWN8NT\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Font 2</a></li>\n</ul><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">1.</span> How to Start Creating a Flyer Template<br>\n</h2><p>First, create a new file. To create a new file, go to <strong>File &gt; New</strong> and set the <strong>Width </strong>to <strong>4 in</strong>, <strong>Height </strong>to <strong>6 in</strong>, and <strong>Resolution </strong>to <strong>300 px/in</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"how to start creating party flyer templates psd\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-new-file.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">2.</span> How to Create Guidelines for a Photoshop Template</h2><p>In this section, we are going to create guidelines for our Photoshop flyer template. Press <strong>Control-R</strong> on your keyboard to show the <strong>Rulers</strong>. Then, using the <strong>Move Tool (V)</strong>, click and drag from the ruler to the canvas to create a new guide. Create four guides and position each <strong>0.25</strong> <strong>in</strong> away from the canvas.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating guidelines for photoshop flyer templates\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-guidelines.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">3.</span> How to Create the Background</h2><h3>Step 1<br>\n</h3><p>In this section, we're going to create the background.  Go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Fill Layer &gt; Solid Color</strong> to create a new solid color fill layer, name it <strong>Background Color</strong>, and choose the color <code class=\"inline\">#161e42</code> as shown below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new solid color fill layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-new-solid-color-fill-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Now <strong>right-click</strong> on this layer and choose <strong>Blending Options</strong>. Then, select and check the <strong>Gradient Overlay</strong> style and use the settings below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adjusting blending options\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adjusting-blending-options.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">4.</span> How to Add Photos and Apply a Photoshop Action<br>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we're going to add photos to the design and apply a Photoshop action to one of them. Go to <strong>File &gt; Open</strong>, select the<strong> </strong>photo from the first stock photo link, and click <strong>Open</strong>.<strong> </strong>Then, press <strong>Control-Shift-N</strong> on your keyboard to create a new layer and name it <strong>brush</strong>. After that, while the <strong>brush</strong>\n layer is selected, brush over the subject with a color. You can also \nmake a selection of the subject and fill the selection with a color \ninstead.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"brushing over subject\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/brushing-over-subject-2.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2<br>\n</h3><p>Now select the <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/energy-photoshop-action-WHRLM97\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Energy Photoshop Action</a> and click on the <strong>Play </strong>button. After the action has finished, customize the effect as you like. I've hidden most of the adjustment layers to avoid stacking adjustments, as we are going to add these on top of the flyer template later. You can check out the<strong> </strong>video\n tutorial (link included in the action help file) for a demonstration of\n how to use the action and also how to customize the results to get the most out of the effect.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"applying energy photoshop action\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/applying-energy-photoshop-action.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3<br>\n</h3><p>Go to <strong>File &gt; Save &gt; Save As</strong> and save the design as a <strong>JPG</strong> file. Then, return to the flyer file, go to <strong>File &gt; Place Embedded</strong>, select the<strong> </strong>photo that you just saved, and click <strong>Place</strong>. Set the <strong>Width </strong>and <strong>Height</strong> of the photo to <strong>41.21%</strong>, position it as shown below, and name this layer <strong>Photo_1</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"placing stock photo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/placing-stock-photo.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Now go to <strong>Layer &gt; Layer Mask &gt; Reveal All</strong> to add the layer mask that reveals the whole layer. Then, choose the <strong>Brush Tool (B)</strong>, pick a soft brush, and set the foreground color to <code class=\"inline\">#000000</code>. While the layer mask is selected, brush as shown below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding layer mask\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adding-layer-mask-5.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 5</h3><p>Select the <strong>Background Color</strong> layer, go to <strong>File &gt; Place Embedded</strong>, select the<strong> </strong>photo from the second stock photo link, and click <strong>Place</strong>. Then, set the <strong>Width </strong>and <strong>Height</strong> of the photo to <strong>17.86%</strong>, position it as shown below, and name this layer <strong>Photo_2</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"placing stock photo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/placing-stock-photo-2.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 6</h3><p>Now go to <strong>Layer &gt; Layer Mask &gt; Reveal All</strong> to add the layer mask that reveals the whole layer. Then, choose the <strong>Brush Tool (B)</strong>, pick a soft brush, and set the foreground color to <code class=\"inline\">#000000</code>. While the layer mask is selected, brush as shown below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding layer mask\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adding-layer-mask-4.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 7</h3><p>Select the current layer thumbnail, go to <strong>Image &gt; Adjustments &gt; Hue/Saturation</strong> to adjust the hue/saturation of this layer, and set the <strong>Saturation</strong> to <strong>-50</strong>. Then, change the <strong>Blending Mode</strong> of this layer to <strong>Hard Light</strong> and set the <strong>Opacity </strong>to <strong>75%</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adjusting hue and saturation\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adjusting-hue-and-saturation-2.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">5.</span> How to Create the Light Source in the PSD Flyer Template<br>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we are going to create the light source. Select the <strong>Photo_1</strong> layer and press <strong>Control-Shift-N</strong> to create a new layer. Then, choose the <strong>Brush Tool (B)</strong>, pick a soft brush, set the <strong>Diameter </strong>of the brush to <strong>1400 px</strong>, and set the foreground color to <code class=\"inline\">#f000ff</code>. Brush as shown below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"brushing into layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/brushing-into-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Change the <strong>Blending Mode</strong> of this layer to <strong>Linear Dodge (Add)</strong> and set the <strong>Opacity </strong>to <strong>40%</strong>. Name this layer <strong>Light Source</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"changing blending mode and opacity\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/changing-blending-mode-and-opacity.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">6.</span> How to Place the Texture</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we're going to place the texture. Go to <strong>File &gt; Place Embedded</strong>, select the<strong> </strong>texture file attached, and click <strong>Place</strong>. Set the <strong>Width </strong>and <strong>Height</strong> of the texture to <strong>100%</strong>, position it as shown below, and name this layer <strong>Texture</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"placing texture\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/placing-texture.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Change the <strong>Blending Mode</strong> of this layer to <strong>Overlay</strong> and set the <strong>Opacity </strong>to <strong>10%</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"changing blending mode and opacity\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/changing-blending-mode-and-opacity-3.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">7.</span> How to Add Text to the Photoshop Flyer Template<br>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we're going to add the text information. Choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong>, set the font to <strong>Fira Sans</strong>, font style to <strong>Bold</strong> for the first part and <strong>Light</strong> for the second part of the text, font size to <strong>30 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option and set the <strong>Tracking </strong>to <strong>100</strong>.  After that, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text below, and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 601.50 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 90.61 px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-text-layer-10.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p><strong>Right-click</strong> on this layer and choose <strong>Blending Options</strong>. Then, select and check the <strong>Drop Shadow</strong> style and use the settings below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adjusting blending options\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adjusting-blending-options-2.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p> Select the <strong>Texture </strong>layer, choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong>, and set the font to <strong>Golden Arrow</strong>, font size to <strong>385 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option. After that, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text below, and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 600.25 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 1134.36 px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-text-layer-2.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Press <strong>Control-J</strong> on your keyboard to duplicate this layer. Then, <strong>Right-click</strong> on this new layer, choose <strong>Convert to Smart Object</strong>, and drag it just below the <strong>Party</strong> layer in the <strong>Layers </strong>panel. After that, go to <strong>Filter &gt; Blur &gt; Gaussian Blur</strong>, set the <strong>Radius</strong> to <strong>10 px</strong>, and name this layer <strong>Glow_1</strong>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding gaussian blur filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adding-gaussian-blur-filter.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 5</h3><p>Press <strong>Control-J</strong> to duplicate this layer. Then, \ndrag this new layer just below the <strong>Glow_1</strong> layer in the <strong>Layers </strong>panel. After that, go to <strong>Filter &gt; Blur &gt; Radial Blur</strong>, and set the <strong>Amount</strong> to <strong>50</strong>, <strong>Blur Method</strong> to <strong>Zoom</strong>, and <strong>Quality</strong> to <strong>Best</strong>. Name this layer <strong>Glow_2</strong>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding radial blur filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adding-radial-blur-filter.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 6</h3><p>Now select the <strong>Party</strong> layer. Choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong> and set the font to <strong>Fira Sans</strong>, font style to <strong>Regular</strong>, font size to <strong>45 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Left</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option. After that, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text below, and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 426.75 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 958.94  px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-text-layer-3.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 7</h3><p>Select the <strong>Texture</strong> layer. Choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong> and set the font to <strong>Fira Sans</strong>, font style to <strong>Light</strong>, font size to <strong>65 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option and set the <strong>Tracking</strong> to <strong>235</strong>. After that, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text below, and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 608.74 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 1314.73 px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-text-layer-4.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 8</h3><p>Now select the <strong>Texture</strong> layer. Choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong> and set the font to <strong>Fira Sans</strong>, font style to <strong>Regular</strong>, font size to <strong>45 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option<strong></strong>. After that, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text below, and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X: 599 px</strong> and <strong>Y: 1424.94 px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-text-layer-5.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 9</h3><p>Select the <strong>Texture</strong> layer and choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong>. Set the font to <strong>Fira Sans</strong>, font style to <strong>Light</strong>, font size to <strong>30 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option and set the <strong>Tracking</strong> to <strong>100</strong><strong></strong>. After that, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text below, and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X:</strong> <strong>601.10</strong> <strong>px</strong> and <strong>Y:</strong> <strong>1474.85</strong> <strong>px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-text-layer-8.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 10</h3><p>Select the <strong>Texture</strong> layer again, and choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong>. Set the font to <strong>Golden Arrow</strong>, font size to <strong>104 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option<strong></strong><strong></strong>. After that, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text below, and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X:</strong> <strong>600</strong> <strong>px</strong> and <strong>Y:</strong> <strong>1569.71</strong> <strong>px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-text-layer-7.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 11</h3><p>Select the <strong>Texture</strong> layer, choose the <strong>Horizontal Type Tool (T)</strong>, and set the font to <strong>Fira Sans</strong>, font style to <strong>Light</strong>, font size to <strong>30 px</strong>, alignment to<strong> Center</strong>, and color to <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>. Then, in the <strong>Character</strong> panel, check the <strong>All Caps</strong> option and set the <strong>Tracking</strong> to <strong>200</strong>. After that, click anywhere inside the canvas, type the text below, and position this layer with the coordinates <strong>X:</strong> <strong>604</strong> <strong>px</strong> and <strong>Y:</strong> <strong>1717.61</strong> <strong>px</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating text layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-text-layer-9.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">8.</span> How to Add the Sound Wave</h2><p>In this section, we're going to add the sound wave. Open the sound wave AI file in Adobe Illustrator, select the top sound wave shape, and press <strong>Control-C</strong> to copy it. Return to the Photoshop flyer file, select the top layer in the <strong>Layers </strong>panel, and press <strong>Control-V</strong> to paste it as a shape layer. Then, press <strong>Control-T</strong> to open up the transform options and set the <strong>Width </strong>and <strong>Height </strong>of the layer to <strong>45.78%</strong>. After that, <strong>Double-click</strong> on this layer thumbnail, choose the color <code class=\"inline\">#ffffff</code>, and name this layer <strong>Sound Wave</strong>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding sound wave\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adding-sound-wave.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">9.</span> How to Make the Final Adjustments to the Party Flyer Template<br>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>In this section, we're going to make some final adjustments to the design. Go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Color Balance</strong> to create a new color balance adjustment layer and name it <strong>Color_Look_1</strong>. Then, <strong>Double-click</strong> on this layer thumbnail and, in the <strong>Properties</strong> panel, enter the settings below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new color balance adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-new-color-balance-adjustment-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Now select the <strong>Sound Wave</strong> layer, go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Curves</strong> to create a new curves adjustment layer, and name it <strong>Color_Look_2</strong>. Then, <strong>Double-click</strong> on this layer thumbnail, and in the <strong>Properties</strong> panel enter the settings below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new curves adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-new-curves-adjustment-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p>Select the <strong>Color_Look_1</strong> layer and press <strong>D</strong> on your keyboard to reset the swatches. Then, go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Gradient Map</strong> to create a new gradient map adjustment layer and name it <strong>Overall Contrast</strong>. After that, change the <strong>Blending Mode</strong> of this layer to <strong>Soft Light</strong> and set the <strong>Opacity </strong>to <strong>12%</strong>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new gradient map adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-new-gradient-map-adjustment-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Now go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Hue/Saturation</strong> to create a new hue/saturation adjustment layer and name it <strong>Overall Saturation</strong>. Then, <strong>Double-click</strong> on this layer thumbnail and, in the<strong> Properties</strong> panel, set the <strong>Saturation</strong> to <strong>+20</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new hue and saturation adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-new-hue-and-saturation-adjustment-layer-2.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 5</h3><p>Go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Levels </strong>to create a new levels adjustment layer, and name it <strong>Overall Brightness</strong>. Then, <strong>Double-click</strong> on this layer thumbnail and, in the <strong>Properties</strong> panel, enter the settings below:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating new levels adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/creating-new-levels-adjustment-layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 6</h3><p>Press <strong>Control-Alt-Shift-E</strong> on your keyboard to make a screenshot, and then press <strong>Control-Shift-U</strong> to desaturate this layer. Then, go to <strong>Filter &gt; Other &gt; High Pass</strong> and set the <strong>Radius</strong> to <strong>2 px</strong>. After that, change the <strong>Blending Mode</strong> of this layer to <strong>Vivid Light</strong> and name it <strong>Overall Sharpening</strong>.<br></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding high pass filter\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/adding-high-pass-filter.jpg\"></figure><h2>You Made It!</h2><p>Congratulations, you have \nsucceeded! You've learned how to create a party flyer Photoshop template. \nHere is our \nfinal result:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"final result\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1437/posts/35524/image/final-result.jpg\"></figure><p>Did you like this party flyer templates PSD design tutorial? Navigate to the </b><a href=\"https://placeit.net/twitch-templates?page=2&amp;f_types=image&amp;f_devices=Twitch%20Panel%20Maker&amp;f_tags=Tw...%2CTwitch%20Templates\" target=\"_self\">Twitch Panel Maker</a><b> at Placeit.</b><strong><br></strong></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/twitch-templates?page=2&amp;f_types=image&amp;f_devices=Twitch%20Panel%20Maker&amp;f_tags=Tw...%2CTwitch%20Templates\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"How to Make Twitch Panels Quickly and Easily\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34139/image/Screenshot%202019-10-26%20at%208.51.40%20am%20copy.jpg\"></a><figcaption><br></figcaption></figure><p><strong>2. Review the Twitch panel templates on offer and select the one you like the most.</strong><br></p><p>For our example, I will teach you how to make a donation panel on Twitch.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34139/image/No1.jpg\"></figure><p><strong>3. To create Twitch panels, use the Twitch panel creator to customise the template provided.</strong></p><ul><li>Starting with the controls on the left, you can add your own text and change the font style and colour.</li></ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34139/image/Screenshot%202019-10-26%20at%208.57.32%20am%20copy.jpg\"></figure><p><strong>4. Move to the controls on the right</strong></p><ul><li>You can now change your background colour and the colour of the line dividing the image. </li></ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34139/image/Screenshot%202019-10-26%20at%208.58.13%20am%20copy.jpg\"></figure><ul><li>Next, you can change the icon used in the panel by uploading your own or using one of those provided by the template. You can also change the colour of the icon here. </li></ul><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34139/image/Screenshot%202019-10-26%20at%208.58.50%20am%20copy.jpg\"></figure><p><strong>5. When you're done, hit the Download button</strong></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/34139/image/Screenshot%202019-10-26%20at%208.59.02%20am%20copy.jpg\"></figure><p>Once you’re satisfied with your design, hit the download button at the top of the screen and download your custom Twitch panel for a small fee. </p><p><strong>If you regularly need to create banners, logos, flyers, posters, social media banners, etc., then the monthly plan may be the best deal for you. </strong></p><p>That’s how to make Twitch panels in five simple steps. 327b58b.webp","http://audio.tutsplus.com.feedsportal.com/c/35227/f/668805/s/34139/sc/4/mf.gif":null,"http://da.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/34139/a2.img":null,"http://pi.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/34139/a2t.img":null},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598925154485},{"createdTime":"2020-09-01 09:52:34","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 09:52:34","title":"How to Make a Pastel Duotone Effect in Photoshop","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/tutorials/how-to-make-a-pastel-duotone-effect-in-photoshop--cms-35534","description":"<figure class=\"final-product final-product--image\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/final_image/How%20to%20create%20pastel%20duotone%20effect%20in%20Photoshop%20main%20preview%20image.jpg\" alt=\"Final product image\"><!--googleoff: index--><figcaption>What You'll Be Creating</figcaption><!--googleon: index--></figure><p>You can create a duotone photo effect in a few simple clicks using a duotone Photoshop action or create it manually with adjustment layers. In this duotone tutorial, I will show how you how to create a duotone effect in Photoshop using adjustment layers.</p><p>If you want to learn these techniques via video, check out our lesson on the <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/user/TutsPremium\" target=\"_self\">Envato Tuts+ YouTube channel</a>:</p><figure data-video-embed=\"true\" data-original-url=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZZ4P9nLr0K8\" class=\"embedded-video\">\n  <iframe src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/ZZ4P9nLr0K8?rel=0\" webkitallowfullscreen=\"webkitallowfullscreen\" mozallowfullscreen=\"mozallowfullscreen\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\" frameborder=\"0\"></iframe>\n</figure><h2>What You'll Learn in This Photoshop Duotone Tutorial</h2><ul>\n<li>How to create a duotone palette<br>\n</li>\n<li>How to make an image duotone in Photoshop using Adjustment Layers</li>\n</ul><h2>Tutorial Assets</h2><p>You'll need the following resource in order to complete this tutorial:</p><ul><li><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/woman-disable-sitting-on-wheelchair-at-beach-HALDN25\" target=\"_self\">Photo</a></li></ul><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">1.</span> <b>How to Create a Duotone Palette</b>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>First of all, let's open our image. Go to <strong>File &gt; Open</strong> or just hit <strong>Control-O </strong>and select the image you want to use.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"opening the image in Photoshop\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/Opening%20image%20in%20photoshop.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Now we can create swatches for easy access to colors. To open the <strong>Swatches </strong>panel, go to <strong>Window &gt; Swatches.</strong></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"opening the swatches panel\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/opening%20the%20swatches%20panel.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p>Open the <strong>Color Picker</strong> and use the following <strong>Color Code</strong>: <code class=\"inline\">#604e74</code>. Once you've entered the code, hit <strong>Add to Swatches.</strong></p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating a color swatch\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/creating%20a%20color%20swatch.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Let's add the second color to our swatches using the following <strong>Color Code</strong>: <code class=\"inline\">#fcf9d7</code>. Our little color palette is ready for creating a duotone Photoshop effect, but you can easily add more pastel colors the same way if you want to try different variations.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"adding the second color code\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/adding%20the%20second%20color%20code.jpg\"></figure><h2>\n<span class=\"sectionnum\">2.</span> <b>How to Make a Duotone Photoshop Image Using Adjustment Layers</b>\n</h2><h3>Step 1</h3><p>Before creating the duotone effect adjustment layer, let's create a channel mixer layer to make the image a bit darker and save the skin color. Go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Channel</strong> <strong>Mixer</strong> and use the <strong>Black &amp; White with Blue Filter </strong>preset.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating a channel mixer layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/creating%20a%20channel%20mixer%20layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 2</h3><p>Change the <strong>Opacity</strong> of this layer to <strong>20%</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"changing the opacity of the layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/changing%20the%20opacity%20of%20the%20adjustment%20layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 3</h3><p>To finish the color correction, add a <strong>Brightness/Contrast</strong> adjustment layer with the following settings: <strong>Brightness: -15</strong>; <strong>Contrast: 25</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating brightness and contrast adjustment layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/creating%20brightness%20and%20contrast%20adjustment%20layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 4</h3><p>Now let's create a duotone photo effect using a gradient map. Go to <strong>Layer &gt; New Adjustment Layer &gt; Gradient Map</strong> and create a gradient with the colors from our palette.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"creating a gradient map layer\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/creating%20a%20gradient%20map%20layer.jpg\"></figure><h3>Step 5</h3><p>And for the last step, change the <strong>Location</strong> of the first point to <strong>10%</strong> and the second point to <strong>95%</strong>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"changing the locations of the points of the colors \" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/changing%20the%20locations%20of%20the%20points%20of%20the%20colors.jpg\"></figure><h2>Awesome Work, You're Now Done!</h2><p>In this simple way, we can create a duotone Photoshop effect using a few adjustment layers and a pastel color palette. This combination gives us a great faded look with an atmospheric vintage feel. If you need any help with the techniques we covered, feel free to contact me!</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"how to create pastel duotone effect in photoshop final result\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/how%20to%20create%20pastel%20duotone%20effect%20in%20photoshop%20final%20result.jpg\"></figure><p>Today we've learned how to make an image duotone in Photoshop, but if you are looking for a super fast and easy way to create this kind of effect, check our list of duotone effect Photoshop actions available on <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com\" target=\"_self\">Envato Elements</a>:</p><h3><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/50-duotone-actions-RZ2ABZ\" target=\"_self\">50 Duotone Actions</a></h3><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/50-duotone-actions-RZ2ABZ\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"50 Duotone Actions\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1381/posts/35534/image/50%20Duotone%20Actions.jpg\"></a></figure><p>This pack of duotone effect Photoshop actions contains 50 instant effects with different well-combined colors. As you can see, hats are a great way to show off your logo design while making a style statement too! All you need to do is upload the logo image, and Placeit will instantly arrange and format it to match this logo <a href=\"https://placeit.net/hat-mockup-generator\" target=\"_self\">hat mockup</a>.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Fantasy Football Logo Hats\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32485/image/Preview%20image%202.jpg\"><figcaption>Add your newly created logo to a signature hat in just a few clicks.</figcaption></figure><h3>3. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/mockups/stages/mockup-of-a-coffee-mug-floating-mid-air-24491\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Fantasy Football Logo Mugs</a>\n</h3><p>Get pumped for your next big game even as you get your shot of caffeine, thanks to fantasy football logo mugs from Placeit. Choose from a variety of styles and orientations, and be sure to explore changes to the color palettes as well. Mugs make great gifts and stay useful long after football season is over.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"Fantasy Football Logo Mugs\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/151/posts/32485/image/Preview%20image%203.jpg\"><figcaption>Help your fans start every day thinking about your team with a cup of coffee and a commemorative mug.</figcaption></figure><h3>4. <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/mockups/stages/mockup-of-a-sporty-man-holding-a-duffle-bag-23061\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Fantasy Football Logo Bags</a>\n</h3><p>By placing your new fantasy team logo on a bag, you can quite literally carry your team with you, wherever you go. Placeit has a variety of bag mockups, and this one strikes the perfect balance of style and utility. Use these to visualize design concepts that you can bring to life in order to share your winning team with family, friends, and everyone you meet!<br></p><h2>Fantasy Football Logos From Envato Elements</h2><p>Placeit is now part of Envato, which offers other incredible resources for design projects. Every item on Elements is available for unlimited download for a single low monthly fee. And as you can see, Elements has thousands of options for your fantasy football logo design. Be sure to explore these as you work to build the best branding for your fantasy team.
