.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn76@2020_1/2020/09/01/01-52-40-810_a4ba76e04a23dbae.webp","https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1823/profiles/20333/profileImage/Profile.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn1@2020_6/2020/09/01/01-52-49-488_763dccd72baf4566.webp","http://audio.tutsplus.com.feedsportal.com/c/35227/f/668805/s/35488/sc/4/mf.gif":null,"http://da.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/35488/a2.img":null,"http://pi.feedsportal.com/r/186529796139/u/407/f/668805/c/35227/s/35488/a2t.img":null},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598925154489},{"createdTime":"2020-09-01 09:52:34","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 09:52:34","title":"How to Make Your Own Logo Design (Do It Yourself Guide)","link":"https://design.tutsplus.com/articles/how-to-make-your-own-logo--cms-32276","description":"<p>So you want to make your own logo. Well, you’ve come to the right place. Though often simple in style, logos are deceptively difficult to create. That’s because they’re not just a combination of pretty graphics with fancy fonts, but actual symbols used to identify a business.</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><img alt=\"make your own logo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/988/posts/32276/image/how-to-make-a-logo.jpg\"><figcaption>Here's an example of the type of business logo you can design with the <a href=\"https://placeit.net/?search=business%20logo\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Placeit Logo Maker.</a></figcaption></figure><p>Making your own logo may sound quite daunting if it’s your first time trying to make your own logo, but we’re here to guide you every step of the way. We'll also direct you to some easy-to-use logo template resources to help you make your own logo. Resources such as <a href=\"https://placeit.net/?search=business%20logo\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Placeit's Logo Maker</a> and <a href=\"https://placeit.net/?search=business%20logo\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">business logo templates</a> from Envato Elements will help you design your own logo quickly and professionally.</p><p>Follow along with us over on our <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/user/TutsPremium\" target=\"_self\">Envato Tuts+ YouTube channel</a>:</p><figure data-video-embed=\"true\" data-original-url=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qrBuCLUlLpQ\" class=\"embedded-video\">\n  <iframe src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/qrBuCLUlLpQ?rel=0\" webkitallowfullscreen=\"webkitallowfullscreen\" mozallowfullscreen=\"mozallowfullscreen\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\" frameborder=\"0\"></iframe>\n</figure><h2>Why Are Logos Important?</h2><p> Before we get into how to make a logo, however, it’s worth taking a look at what the qualities of a well-designed logo are. After all, how can you design your own logo if you don’t know what makes a logo a success or a failure?</p><p>One reason logos are important is because they tell potential clients and customers concisely and effectively what a business is all about. Using very specific, carefully thought-out imagery, shapes, colours, and/or fonts, they make a business instantly recognisable and differentiate it from any other company in their market. Logos are part of a brand's visual identity, and as such, creating an effective logo requires thought, research, planning, and creativity.</p><h2>5 Qualities to Aim for When You Design Your Own Logo</h2><p>No matter what kind of business you’re designing a logo for, there are five key qualities all well-designed logos have in common, which you should be familiar with and aim for as you start to make your own logo. (<em>Each of these examples is from the </em><a href=\"https://placeit.net/?search=business%20logo\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><em>Placeit Logo Maker</em></a><em>.</em>)</p><h3>1. Simplicity </h3><p>This is key when creating a successful logo. A simple logo is easy to recognise and remember, as well as easy to use in a variety of media. Here's an illustration of simplicity in a logo:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/gift-shop-logo-maker-with-two-colors-1395c?checkboxText_T3=false\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"how to create your own logo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20make%20a%20logo7.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>2. Relevance </h3><p>Through the colours and imagery you use, your logo should reflect the image you want your company to convey. You make sure your logo is relevant when it gives viewers a good idea of what your business is all about. Notice the medical symbolism in this psychoanalyst's logo:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/counselling-logo-maker-with-a-creative-medical-art-1522b?colorText_T1=#073763&amp;colorText_T4=%23073763&amp;colorFolder_Inner%20Graphic=%230b5394&amp;colorSolidColor_Color=%239fc5e8\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"how to create your own logo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20make%20a%20logo8.jpg\"></a> </figure><h3>3. Timelessness</h3><p>Your logo should avoid being so trendy that it looks dated 10 or 50 years from the day you put the finishing touches to it. Here's a logo sample with a classic look:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/abstract-logo-template-for-architects-1420e\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"how to create your own logo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20make%20a%20logo10.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>4. Memorability</h3><p>The whole point of your logo is to identify and differentiate a brand, capture the viewer’s attention, and leave a positive and lasting impression. It stands to reason, therefore, that the best logos must be memorable. It's hard to forget the bird symbol on this logo:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/woodworking-logo-template-1550c\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"how to create your own logo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20make%20a%20logo3.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>5. Versatility </h3><p>Logos need to be versatile because they need to work across a variety of media. You should be able to scale them down or up, use them in print or on the web, and they should look great under any circumstances. This black and white logo with a touch of gold is very versatile: </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/craft-suppliers-logo-template-1277b?graphicFolder_Graphic=44\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"how to create your own logo\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20make%20a%20logo9.jpg\"></a></figure><p>Now that you're clear about the five qualities your logo should have, let’s look at how to make a logo. </p><h2>How to Create Your Own Logo in 5 Simple Steps</h2><p>Before you learn how to create your own logo, it's important to understand that logos come in three basic forms:</p><ol>\n<li>An abstract symbol like the Nike swoosh or Apple’s bitten apple. </li>\n<li>An illustrative symbol that indicates exactly what the company does, like a vacuum cleaner for a house-cleaning service or a loaf of bread for a bakery. </li>\n<li>A font-based logo like those used by the makers of Coca Cola and Barbie that use distinct type treatments to make the font unique to the brand. </li>\n</ol><p>Most companies use a font-based logo to support an abstract or illustrative symbol, a combination which makes logos much easier to remember. </p><p>Now let’s get down to the nuts and bolts of how to create your own logo. I like this sample from the <a href=\"https://placeit.net/?search=business%20logo\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Placeit Logo Maker</a>:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/logo-maker-for-interior-design-studio-1325d\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"How to Create Your Own Logo in 5 Simple Steps\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/Screen%20Shot%202018-11-26%20at%2018.57.24%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>1. Get Clear About Your Design Goals</h3><p>The first step you need to take in your do-it-yourself logo design venture is to select a sheet of paper and:</p><ul>\n<li>Write a column of adjectives that describe your brand and the benefits it offers. Think of words like modern, fun, lively, healthy, calming, wholesome, reliable, funky, etc. Let yourself free associate.</li>\n<li>Now start another column on the same sheet of paper and write a list or sketch symbols you think best capture your brand and the benefits it offers. They could be abstract or literal, representing an idea or an object. Again, let yourself free associate. Nothing is off limits at this point.</li>\n<li>Next, pull out your paints, coloured pencils, or pens, and in another column on the same sheet of paper create some colour swatches that reflect the adjectives you used in the first column. For example, if you wrote fun and lively, then select colours you associate with being fun and lively. Likewise, if you wrote adjectives like calming and wholesome, select colours you associate with those adjectives. </li>\n</ul><p>The colours on this sample logo seem calming:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/real-estate-logo-maker-for-b-b-969e?checkboxText_T3=false\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"How to Create Your Own Logo in 5 Simple Steps\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/Screen%20Shot%202018-11-26%20at%2019.03.12%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>2. Study the Competition</h3><p>Now, study the logos used by your competition and ask yourself what makes their design a success or failure. Think about how to create your own logo differently from theirs. </p><h3>3. Get Inspired</h3><p>Study the logos of successful brands that you like outside your business area and ask yourself what makes their logo stand out.</p><ul>\n<li>Does the logo use lines, shapes, images, or illustrations? What do they communicate about the brand? How do they communicate their message?</li>\n<li>If the logo is font-based, is the font serif or sans serif? What makes the font interesting or different? What does it communicate? Fun, stability, innovation, or something else?</li>\n<li>If the logo is a combination of symbol and font, how do the two work together? Does one frame the other in some way, or are they overlapping, stacked, or adjacent?</li>\n<li>Look at the colours used and note the effect they have on you as a viewer. Are they vibrant and exciting, serious and sedate, or calming and down to earth? </li>\n<li>How is negative space used to complement and show off the design?</li>\n<li>How can you incorporate the best qualities from these brands into your own design?</li>\n</ul><p>What do you think of when you see the colours on this sample logo? (<em>Sample from the </em><a href=\"https://placeit.net/?search=business%20logo\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\"><em>Placeit Logo Maker</em></a><em>.</em>)</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/logo-maker-for-fashion-stylists-1311c?graphicFolder_Graphic=60&amp;colorSolidColor_Color=%23c27ba0\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"How to Create Your Own Logo in 5 Simple Steps\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/Screen%20Shot%202018-11-26%20at%2018.58.55%20copy.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>4. Design Your Own Logo </h3><p>Now it’s time to focus on how to design your own logo. Review the notes you made in step one and circle the best ideas from each of the three columns. Select one idea from each column and do a rough sketch bearing in mind everything you’ve learnt from researching your competition and inspiration. If you’re proficient in Adobe Illustrator, at this point you may want to switch to this program to resolve your ideas there. </p><p>Unfortunately, this step is where most people get stuck. So if you do, don’t worry—later on, we’ll go through a couple of simple tools and templates you can use to create a unique, beautifully designed logo with little to no design skills required! </p><p>You could make your own logo similar to this sample with the help of a <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/graphic-templates/logos\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">logo maker tool</a>:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/organic-food-restaurant-logo-maker-1236b\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"How to Create Your Own Logo in 5 Simple Steps\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/Design%20Your%20Own%20Logo.jpg\"></a></figure><h3>5. Reflect and Revise </h3><p>When you think you’ve finished your design, put it away and take a break for an hour to a few days. Return to your design after your break with fresh eyes. Remove any elements that don’t fit with your logo design goals and make any tweaks to the design you deem necessary. At this point, you can have a trusted friend or colleague look at the design and give you feedback. Ask them:</p><ul>\n<li>What business do they think the logo belongs to?</li>\n<li>What adjectives they would use to describe the business based on the logo?</li>\n<li>What values do they think the logo communicates about the business?</li>\n<li>How do they feel when they look at the logo?</li>\n</ul><p>These are all questions designed to uncover whether you've achieved your objective with the logo or if you need to make some adjustments.</p><p>Make any additional changes that are necessary to help your logo communicate effectively. And once that’s done, you’re ready to go live.</p><h2>How to Design Your Own Logo Online</h2><p>If you don’t draw or in spite of the ideas and prompts you jotted down in step 1, you find yourself staring at the blank paper not knowing where to start, a logo maker can help.</p><p>A <a href=\"https://placeit.net/online-logo-maker\" target=\"_self\">logo maker</a> like this one at Placeit is a do-it-yourself logo design generator: </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/online-logo-maker\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"Placeit logo maker\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20design%20your%20own%20logo%20online1%20copy.jpg\"></a><figcaption><a href=\"https://placeit.net/online-logo-maker\" rel=\"external\" target=\"_blank\">Design your own logo</a> with the help of the Placeit logo maker tool.</figcaption></figure><p>This tool was created specifically for novice logo designers who may not yet have developed the skills needed to know how to make a logo or for more experienced designers who need a bit of help with fast-turn-around jobs. </p><p>A logo maker provides you with a wide choice of logo templates which you can easily customise by tweaking the graphics, fonts, and colours to make your own logo.</p><p>Say you want to create a logo for your or a client’s photography business. Well, just follow these five simple steps to discover how to design your own logo online in a matter of minutes.  </p><h3>1. Navigate to <a href=\"https://placeit.net\" target=\"_self\">Placeit.net</a> and sign up for FREE!</h3><p>Once you've signed up for Placeit, you can create an account and log in to it:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"do it yourself logo design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20design%20your%20own%20logo%20online1a%20copy.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Log in to your Placeit account to begin creating a do-it-yourself logo design.</figcaption></figure><h3>2. Browse the Logo Templates </h3><p>Enter the name of the business you’re creating the logo for and search for your industry by clicking the drop-down menu in the search bar that says <strong>All Industries</strong>. </p><p>Say you're creating a logo for a photographer called Mona Smalls. Just type her name in the bar and select <strong>Photographer</strong> from the drop-down menu. All the templates designed specifically for photographers will appear with the name Mona Smalls on them. </p><p>Browse the templates and select the one that most appeals to you:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/online-logo-maker\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"do it yourself logo design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20design%20your%20own%20logo%20online%201b.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Here's an example of photography templates customised with the name you chose.</figcaption></figure><h4>3. Open the Logo Maker </h4><p>When you click on your chosen template, it'll open up in the logo maker. For my example, I chose the <a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/photography-logo-maker-a1196?fontText_T1=Alice%20Regular\">Design a Photography Logo</a> template shown here:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/photography-logo-maker-a1196?fontText_T1=Alice%20Regular\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"do it yourself logo design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20design%20your%20own%20logo%20online%202%20copy.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Choose the template design that best fits your needs.</figcaption></figure><h3>4. Customise Your Logo Template</h3><p>You can now customise your logo template as much or as little as you like, based on the adjectives and colours you identified in Step 1. The adjectives I’m using for this photography business are feminine, modern, and calm. </p><p>Starting with the controls on the left and working from top to bottom, you can add text and change the font style and colour. I changed the business name to Mona Smalls. Then I changed the font to a more feminine style. Next, I changed the colour of the font to a lavender hue, which I consider both calming and feminine: </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/photography-logo-maker-a1196?fontText_T1=Alice%20Regular\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"do it yourself logo design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20design%20your%20own%20logo%20online%203%20copy.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Notice the new colour and font.</figcaption></figure><p>Moving to the controls on the right and working from top to bottom, you can change the background colour, the graphics, and their colours to ones that better reflect your goals for your logo. </p><p>I wanted a graphic that had a modern touch, so I chose the clean, geometric graphic of an eye with a camera shutter inside it, which gives me a modern spin on familiar camera iconography. Then I changed the colour of the icon to reflect my colour scheme. Finally, I removed the background colour from the logo as I wanted a transparent background that I felt would be more useful on a number of different media: </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/photography-logo-maker-a1196?fontText_T1=Alice%20Regular\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"do it yourself logo design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20design%20your%20own%20logo%20online%204%20copy.jpg\"></a><figcaption>You can make a logo with a transparent background.</figcaption></figure><p>Scrolling down the page, you've got two additional options:</p><ol>\n<li>You can see your selected colours applied to different logo styles for more design inspiration.</li>\n<li>If you get stuck and need even more logo ideas, you can try one of the presets offered. </li>\n</ol><p>Here's a look at some of the photography logo presets:</p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/photography-logo-maker-a1196?fontText_T1=Alice%20Regular\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"do it yourself logo design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20design%20your%20own%20logo%20online%205%20copy.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Presets can help you design your logo if you get stuck.</figcaption></figure><p>Best of all, as you design your own logo, you can make use of the state-of-the-art mockup tool at the bottom of the page, which shows your logo in a range of real-life scenarios:  </p><figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://placeit.net/c/logos/stages/photography-logo-maker-a1196?fontText_T1=Alice%20Regular\" target=\"_self\"><img alt=\"do it yourself logo design\" src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/uploads/users/1631/posts/32276/image/how%20to%20design%20your%20own%20logo%20online%206%20copy.jpg\"></a><figcaption>Use the mockup tool to see your logo design in a real-life scenario.</figcaption></figure><h3>5.
